CANADIAN AND WORLD MINERAL DEPOSIT DATABASES
Geological Survey of Canada

Database name: Canadian U-Th-REE deposits and occurrences
Custodial agency: Geological Survey of Canada
Compilers: S.S. Gandhi, N. Prasad, L.B. Chorlton, C. Richer and D.R. Lentz
Release date: 2015-11-27
   
Description These web reports were extracted from the Canadian U-Th-REE deposit and occurrence database. Locations for many of the deposits were retrieved in the 1980s and 1990s from small scale maps using paper methods and are very approximate. A select few deposits have been located using GIS and satellite imagery, or Google Earth, and are more accurately located.
